# <a name="office-365-operated-by-21vianet"></a><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-104">21Vianet 運作的 Office 365</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-104">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p102">由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365，是設計用以滿足在中國對於安全性、可靠性和可調整性雲端服務的需求。這項服務由 Microsoft 授權給 21Vianet 的技術提供支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p102">Office 365 operated by 21Vianet is designed to meet the needs for secure, reliable, and scalable cloud services in China. This service is powered by technology that Microsoft has licensed to 21Vianet.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-107">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-107">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p103">Microsoft 不直接營運此項服務。由 21Vianet 營運、提供並管理服務的提供。21Vianet 是中國最大的運營商中立網際網路資料中心服務提供者，提供託管、受管理的網路服務，以及雲端運算基礎結構服務。透過 Microsoft 授權的技術，21Vianet 會營運當地的 Office 365 資料中心，以提供 Office 365 服務，並將資料保留在中國境內。21Vianet 也提供[訂閱和計費服務以及支援](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=847978
)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p103">Microsoft does not operate the service itself. 21Vianet operates, provides, and manages delivery of the service. 21Vianet is the largest carrier-neutral Internet data center services provider in China, providing hosting, managed network services, and cloud computing infrastructure services. By licensing Microsoft technologies, 21Vianet operates local Office 365 datacenters to provide the ability to use Office 365 services while keeping data within China. 21Vianet also provides [subscription and billing services, as well as support](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=847978
).</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
>  <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-113">這些服務須遵守中國法律。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-113">These services are subject to Chinese laws.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p104">由於中國服務的獨特本質 (由合作夥伴從中國內部的資料中心營運)，可能尚未啟用部分功能。經過一段時間後，客戶將會看到服務的功能逐漸完整。有關的差異，請參閱服務描述註腳。如需更高層級的差異概觀，請參閱[深入了解由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=846725)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p104">Due to the unique nature of the China services—operated by a partner from datacenters inside China—there are some features that have not yet been enabled. Customers will see the services come closer to full feature parity over time. See the service description footnotes for differences. For a higher-level overview of differences, see [Learn about Office 365 operated by 21Vianet](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?linkid=846725).</span></span>
  
## <a name="service-availability-within-each-plan"></a><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-118">每個方案中可用的服務</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-118">Service availability within each plan</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p105">每個由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 方案皆包含一些個別服務，例如 Exchange Online 和 SharePoint Online。下表顯示每項 Office 365 方案中可用的服務。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p105">Each Office 365 plan operated by 21Vianet includes a number of individual services, such as Exchange Online and SharePoint Online. The following table shows the services that are available in each Office 365 plan.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-121">由 Office 365 之 21Vianet 版本運作的 Office 365 是專屬於中國的版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-121">The Office 365 operated by 21Vianet version of Office 365 is specific to China.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p106"><sup>1</sup> 包含功能例如 Office 365 管理、Office 365 套件應用程式、使用者帳戶管理、網域、服務健康狀況和持續性、報告、服務更新、說明和訓練、網路等等。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[平台功能](office-365-operated-by-21vianet.md#platform-features)表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p106"><sup>1</sup> Includes features such as Office 365 administration, Office 365 suite apps, user account management, domains, service health and continuity, reporting, service updates, help and training, networking, and so on. > <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-1138"><sup>1</sup> office 365 與 Office 365 的 21vianet 來 21Vianet 不提供支援的任何不受製造商支援的作業系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-1138"><sup>1</sup> Office 365 and Office 365 operated by 21Vianet do not provide support for any operating system that is not supported by its manufacturer.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-1139"><sup>2</sup> 在 由 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 企業版 K1 中，Office 365 影片僅限檢視 (不可發佈或共用)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-1139"><sup>2</sup> In Office 365 Enterprise F1 operated by 21Vianet, Office 365 Video is limited to viewing only (no publishing or sharing).</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-1140"><sup>3</sup>若您使用目錄同步作業與本機 Active Directory，您必須刪除帳戶或使用本機的 Active Directory，而不是 Office 365 入口網站或使用 Windows Azure Active Directory 模組來變更密碼PowerShell。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-1140"><sup>3</sup> If you are using directory synchronization with a local Active Directory, you must delete accounts or change passwords by using the local Active Directory, rather than the Office 365 portal or by using the Azure Active Directory module for Windows PowerShell.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-1141"><sup>4</sup> 尚未在 21Vianet 運作的 Office 365 中提供使用，但即將推出。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-1141"><sup>4</sup> Not yet available in Office 365 operated by 21Vianet, but coming soon.</span></span> 
<br/><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p108"><sup>5</sup>您可以有一個公用網站與 Office 365 除非您已從舊版的 Office 365 升級。在此情況下，您有兩個公用網站，但是只有其中可以裝載以自訂的網域名稱。如需使用適用於 Business 訂閱的兩個網站的詳細資訊，請參閱 ＜ [Work with 您兩種 Office 365 公用網站](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=271589)。如果您有不同的訂閱，深入了解[Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=325009)的公用網站協助公用網站。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p108"><sup>5</sup> You can have only one Public Website with Office 365 unless you've upgraded from an earlier version of Office 365. In that case, you have two Public Websites, but only one of them can be hosted with a custom domain name. For more information about working with the two websites for Business subscriptions, see [Work with your two Office 365 Public Websites](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=271589). If you have a different subscription, learn more about public websites at [Public Website help for Office 365](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkID=325009). </span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p109"><sup>6</sup>減少字詞折扣所購買的基座可能會受限於早期的終止費用。不適用的每月為基礎付費訂閱。></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p109"><sup>6</sup> Reducing seats that were purchased with a term discount may be subject to an early termination fee. This is not applicable for subscriptions paid on a monthly basis. > </span></span><br/><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-1148"><sup>7</sup> office 365 教育版計劃不支援從 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心的授權基座變更：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-1148"><sup>7</sup> Office 365 Education plans do not support license seat changes from the Microsoft 365 admin center:</span></span>
<br/><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p110"><sup>8</sup> Microsoft Sway 沒有目前的客戶的特定地理位置。一些舊版的 Office 365 計劃不再年 8 月 2015年市場可能也無法存取 Microsoft Sway。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p110"><sup>8</sup> Microsoft Sway is not currently available for customers in certain geographies. > <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-2698"><sup>1</sup> 郵件使用者會定義為「信箱」，而且可以連同外部郵件連絡人直接在 Exchange 系統管理中心 (EAC) 中新增、移除或管理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-2698"><sup>1</sup> Mail users are defined as "Mailboxes," and, along with external mail contacts, can be added, removed, and otherwise managed directly in the Exchange admin center (EAC).</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p131"><sup>2</sup> 沒有 RBAC 自訂。僅限系統管理員角色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p131"><sup>2</sup> No RBAC customization. Admin roles only. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p132"><sup>3</sup>可檢視受管理的網域，且可在 EAC 中編輯網域類型。所有其他網域管理必須完成 Microsoft 365 系統管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p132"><sup>3</sup> Managed domains can be viewed and domain types can be edited in the EAC. All other domain management must be done in the Microsoft 365 admin center. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p133"><sup>4</sup>提供彈性的條件和動作不同 EOP 與 Exchange Online 之間。如需可用的條件和動作在 EOP 中的清單，請參閱[傳輸規則條件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320392)和[傳輸規則動作](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320393)。如需可用的準則與 Exchange Online 中的動作的清單，請參閱[傳輸規則條件](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320394)和[傳輸規則動作](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320395)。<sup>5</sup> EOP 稽核報告是 Exchange Online 稽核報告，但不包括信箱的相關資訊的子集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p133"><sup>4</sup> The available flexible criteria and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online. For a list of available criteria and actions in EOP, see [Transport Rule Criteria](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320392) and [Transport Rule Actions](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320393). For a list of available criteria and actions in Exchange Online, see [Transport Rule Criteria](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320394) and [Transport Rule Actions](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320395). <sup>5</sup> EOP auditing reports are a subset of Exchange Online auditing reports that exclude information about mailboxes. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p134"><sup>6</sup>預設內容篩選動作是要將垃圾郵件移至 [收件者的垃圾郵件] 資料夾。這與內部部署信箱搭配使用，您也必須設定兩個 Exchange 傳輸規則來偵測垃圾郵件標頭新增 EOP 的內部部署伺服器上。如需詳細資訊，請參閱[確定垃圾郵件會路由傳送至每一個使用者的垃圾郵件] 資料夾](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320396)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p134"><sup>6</sup> The default content filter action is to move spam messages to the recipients' Junk Email folder. For this to work with on-premises mailboxes, you must also configure two Exchange Transport rules on your on-premises servers to detect spam headers added by EOP. For more information, see [Ensure that Spam is Routed to Each User's Junk Email Folder](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?LinkId=320396). </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-2710"><sup>7</sup> 透過 EOP 篩選其信箱的 Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) 客戶可以使用此功能，而且很快就可以供 Exchange Online 客戶使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-2710"><sup>7</sup> This feature is available to Exchange Server 2013 Service Pack 1 (SP1) customers whose mailboxes are being filtered by EOP, and will soon be available to Exchange Online customers.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-2711"><sup>8</sup> EOP 報告是 Exchange Online 報告的子集，但不包括信箱的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-2711"><sup>8</sup> EOP reports are a subset of Exchange Online reports that exclude information about mailboxes.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-2712"><sup>9</sup> 包括 DLP 報告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-2712"><sup>9</sup> Includes DLP reports.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-2713"><sup>10</sup> 會掃描輸入及輸出郵件，但不掃描從組織中寄件者傳送給組織中收件者的內部郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-2713"><sup>10</sup> Scans inbound and outbound messages, but does not scan internal messages sent from a sender in your organization to a recipient in your organization.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-2714"><sup>11</sup> EOP 與 Exchange Online 可用的述詞和動作各不相同。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-2714"><sup>11</sup> The available predicates and actions differ between EOP and Exchange Online.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-2715"><sup>12</sup> 混合式安裝程式不能透過混合式精靈使用，但您可以手動設定 (如果您有 Exchange SP1)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-2715"><sup>12</sup> Hybrid setup is not available through Hybrid Wizard, but can be set up manually if you have Exchange SP1.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p136"><sup>1</sup> 使用者信箱必須位於 Exchange 2010 SP2 或更新版本上。 > <sup>2</sup>「就地封存」僅可用來封存已套用授權之單一使用者或實體的郵件。禁止使用「就地封存」來儲存來自多個使用者或實體的郵件。例如，IT 系統管理員不能建立共用信箱，再由使用者純粹為了封存的目的來複製 (透過 [副本] 或 [密件副本] 欄位，或透過傳輸規則) 共用信箱。 > <sup>3</sup> 如需支援的 Microsoft Outlook 版本清單，請參閱 [Exchange Online 封存中的用戶端功能](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md)。 > <sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS 是內部部署伺服器，必須個別採購並管理，以便啟用支援的 IRM 功能。 > <sup>5</sup> 當您對信箱進行就地保留或訴訟資料暫留時，會同時保留主要和封存信箱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p136"><sup>1</sup> User mailboxes must reside on Exchange 2010 SP2 or later. > <sup>2</sup> In-Place Archive can only be used to archive mail for a single user or entity for which a license has been applied. Using an In-Place Archive as a means to store mail from multiple users or entities is prohibited. For example, IT administrators can't create shared mailboxes and have users copy (through the Cc or Bcc field, or through a transport rule) a shared mailbox for the explicit purpose of archiving. > <sup>3</sup> For a list of supported Microsoft Outlook versions see [Client Features in Exchange Online Archiving](../exchange-online-archiving-service-description/client-features.md). > <sup>4</sup> Windows Server AD RMS is an on-premises server that must be purchased and managed separately in order to enable the supported IRM features. > <sup>5</sup> When you put a mailbox on In-Place Hold or Litigation Hold, the hold is placed on both the primary and the archive mailbox.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p138"><sup>1</sup>使用資料夾同步處理，您必須具有 Office 2013 或更新版本 (標準版或 Professional edition) 或包含 Office 應用程式的 Office 365 訂閱。Office 365 商務 Essentials、 Office 365 企業版 E1 和 Office 365 教育版的計劃不包含訂閱 Office 桌面應用程式。不過，您可以使用資料夾同步處理如果您有 Office 2013 或稍後安裝和訂閱其中一個計劃。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p138"><sup>1</sup> To use folder sync, you must have Office 2013 or later (Standard or Professional edition) or an Office 365 subscription that includes Office applications. Office 365 Business Essentials, Office 365 Enterprise E1, and Office 365 Education plans do not include subscriptions to Office desktop applications. However, you can use folder sync if you have Office 2013 or later installed and subscribe to one of these plans. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p139"><sup>2</sup> kiosk 帳戶有限 OneDrive for Business 的功能。Kiosk 客戶可以使用 OneDrive for Business 資料夾同步處理用戶端應用程式同步處理共用電腦和存取文件的離線與小組網站文件庫。但 kiosk 帳戶不包括 OneDrive for Business 的個人網站，讓他們不會受益於 OneDrive for Business 個人文件庫與 1 TB 的線上儲存。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p139"><sup>2</sup> Kiosk accounts have limited OneDrive for Business functionality. Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline. But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB of online storage. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4720"><sup>3</sup> 不支援 Access 2010。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4720"><sup>3</sup> Access 2010 is not supported.</span></span>
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4721"><sup>4</sup> 因為 Kiosk 使用者不能是系統管理員，所以有 Kiosk 使用者的租用戶至少必須有一個企業使用者使用者，才能存取系統管理中心。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4721"><sup>4</sup> Because Kiosk users can't be administrators, tenants with Kiosk users need at least one Enterprise user to access the admin center.</span></span>
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4722"><sup>5</sup> SharePoint Online 客戶必須下載並安裝免費的排名模型調整應用程式才能建立及自訂排名模型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4722"><sup>5</sup> SharePoint Online customers need to download and install the free Rank Model Tuning App in order to create and customize ranking models.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4723"><sup>6</sup> 當您使用 eDiscovery 功能時，允許此功能的計劃授權要求會套用至所有屬於 eDiscovery 動作 (搜尋、保留、匯出) 的使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4723"><sup>6</sup> When you use eDiscovery features, the licensing requirement for a plan that permits that feature applies to all end users that are part of the eDiscovery action (Search, Hold, Export).</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4724"><sup>7</sup> 已驗證的 SharePoint Online 使用者可以使用多面向導覽存取私用網站集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4724"><sup>7</sup> Authenticated SharePoint Online users can access private site collections with faceted navigation.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p140"><sup>8</sup> kiosk 使用者不能建立使用 live 並排顯示的 Office 文件。若要建立的文件、 kiosk 使用者必須進行安裝從 SharePoint Online 網站按一下 [**新增]** ，然後從 [**建立新檔案**] 功能表中選取檔案類型-Word 文件、 Excel 活頁簿、 PowerPoint 簡報、 OneNote 筆記本或 Excel 問卷。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p140"><sup>8</sup> Kiosk users cannot create Office documents using live tiles. To create a document, kiosk users must do so from a SharePoint Online site by clicking **New** and then selecting a file type - Word document, Excel workbook, PowerPoint presentation, OneNote notebook, or Excel survey - from the **Create a new file** menu. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4727"><sup>9</sup> 在您的國家/地區中，某些提供者可能被封鎖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4727"><sup>9</sup> Some providers may be blocked in your country/region.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p141"><sup>10</sup> 沙箱化解決方案無法包含使用者程式碼。相反地，它們只能包含定義 (.xml) 檔案，以及伺服器在啟動方案時所處理的資源。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p141"><sup>10</sup> Sandboxed solutions cannot contain user code. Rather, they may only contain definition (.xml) files and resources that are processed by the server when they activate. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p142"><sup>11</sup> 使用電子郵件與組織外的任何人共用文件、程式庫或網站。系統管理員還是能夠將它開啟，但會出現警告訊息，指出它可能在您的國家/地區外進行檔案共用存取。嘗試與組織外部的其他人共用的使用者會收到相同的警告訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p142"><sup>11</sup> Sharing a document, library, or site by email with someone outside of your organization. Administrators do have the ability to turn it on, but will get a warning message indicating that it could make files shared accessible outside of your country. Users who attempt to share with someone outside of the organization will receive the same warning message. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p143"><sup>12</sup> Kiosk 帳戶具有受限的商務用 OneDrive 功能。Kiosk 客戶可以使用商務用 OneDrive 資料夾同步處理用戶端應用程式，將小組網站文件庫與共用電腦進行同步，然後離線存取文件。但是 Kiosk 帳戶並未包含商務用 OneDrive 個人網站，所以無法享有商務用 OneDrive 個人文件庫的 1 TB 或 5 TB 線上儲存空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p143"><sup>12</sup> Kiosk accounts have limited OneDrive for Business functionality. Kiosk customers can use the OneDrive for Business folder sync client application to sync team site document libraries with a shared computer and access documents offline. But kiosk accounts do not include a OneDrive for Business Personal Site, so they do not benefit from a OneDrive for Business personal library with 1 TB or 5 TB of online storage. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p144"><sup>13</sup> 您可以在任何行動瀏覽器中檢視文件。您必須安裝 Office Mobile 應用程式才能編輯文件。Office Mobile 目前可供 Windows Phone 和平板電腦、Android 手機和平板電腦、iPhone 和 iPad 使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p144"><sup>13</sup> You can view documents in any Mobile browser. You need to install the Office Mobile app to edit documents. Office Mobile is currently available for Windows phones and tablets, Android phones and tablets, iPhone, and iPad. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4739"><sup>14</sup> 只有簡體中文和英文版說明。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4739"><sup>14</sup> Help is available only in Simplified Chinese and English.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p145"><sup>15</sup> Visio Online 可以免費使用 (檢視功能)。Visio Online 建立和編輯功能需要授權。如需 Visio Online 的詳細資訊，請參閱＜[Visio Online Service Description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md)＞。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p145"><sup>15</sup> Visio Online consumption (view capability) is available for free. Visio Online create and edit capabilities require a license. For more information about Visio Online, see the [Visio Online Service Description](../visio-online-service-description/visio-online-service-description.md). </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-4743"><sup>16</sup> K1 使用者可存取 SharePoint Server 在混合式設定中，但 Office 365 K1 不包含要存取伺服器; CAL 權限必須另外購買這些權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-4743"><sup>16</sup> K1 users can access SharePoint Server in a hybrid setup, but Office 365 K1 does not include CAL rights to access the server; these rights must be purchased separately.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p148"><sup>1</sup> Skype 商務 (Lync) 用戶端支援搭配下列訂閱選項] 中，但不包含在內。Lync 2013 Basic 是可用的所有客戶。Lync Basic 桌面用戶端是在本機上已安裝的應用程式提供顯示狀態、 立即訊息與會議功能內含 Skype 商務 Online 的 Office 365 計劃。Office 365 ProPlus 和 Office 365 企業版 E3 包含完整的 Skype Business (Lync) 應用程式，其中包含其他功能，例如進階電話語音支援、 封存、 和符合性功能。商務 Online 授權 Skype 必須被指派每位使用者。如需 Lync Basic 功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[Skype for Business Online 用戶端比較表](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p148"><sup>1</sup> The Skype for Business (Lync) client is supported for use with these subscription options, but it is not included. Lync 2013 Basic is available for all customers. The Lync Basic desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging, and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online. Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Enterprise E3 include the full Skype for Business (Lync) application, which includes additional features such as advanced telephony support, archiving, and compliance features. A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user. For more information about Lync Basic features, see [Skype for Business Online client comparison tables](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx). </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-5742">封存的商務 online Skype 倚賴 Exchange 就地保留功能，不包含在此計劃<sup>2</sup> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-5742"><sup>2</sup> Archiving for Skype for Business Online depends upon the Exchange In-Place Hold feature, which is not included in this plan.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-5743"><sup>3</sup> 只能透過商務用 Skype 系統管理中心管理介面進行存取。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-5743"><sup>3</sup> Only accessible through the Skype for Business admin center management interface.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p149"><sup>4</sup>的 Office 365 21vianet 來 21Vianet、 商務用戶端 Skype 支援搭配下列訂閱選項] 中，但不包含在內。若要存取多方視訊 （圖庫檢視）、 OneNote 會議筆記、 錄製及行事曆委派功能，使用者必須擁有完整的 Skype 商務用戶端的權限。您可以取得商務用戶端完整 Skype 購買 Office 2013 Professional Plus。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p149"><sup>4</sup> In Office 365 operated by 21Vianet, the Skype for Business client is supported for use with these subscription options, but it is not included. You can obtain the full Skype for Business client by purchasing Office 2013 Professional Plus. </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-5747"><sup>5</sup>在 Office 365 的 21Vianet 21vianet，有獨立 Skype 對商務計劃的承租人可以存取報告功能如果承租人也有至少一個作用中的 Exchange 授權，例如 Exchange Online 計劃 1 或 Exchange Online 計劃 2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-5747"><sup>5</sup> In Office 365 operated by 21Vianet, tenants with a standalone Skype for Business plan can access reporting features if the tenant also has at least one active Exchange license, such as Exchange Online Plan 1 or Exchange Online Plan 2.</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-p153"><sup>1</sup> Skype 商務 (Lync) 用戶端支援搭配下列訂閱選項] 中，但不包含在內。Lync 2013 Basic 是可用的所有客戶。Lync Basic 桌面用戶端是在本機上已安裝的應用程式提供顯示狀態、 立即訊息與會議功能內含 Skype 商務 Online 的 Office 365 計劃。Office 365 ProPlus 與 Office 365 企業版 E3 包含商務 (Lync) 應用程式的完整 Skype 包括包括進階電話語音支援的其他功能、 封存&amp;符合性功能。商務 Online 授權 Skype 必須被指派每位使用者。如需有關 Lync Basic 功能的詳細資訊，請參閱[Skype for Business Online 用戶端比較表](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-p153"><sup>1</sup> The Skype for Business (Lync) client is supported for use with these subscription options, but it is not included. Lync 2013 Basic is available for all customers. The Lync Basic desktop client is a locally installed application that provides presence, instant messaging and conferencing features for Office 365 plans that include Skype for Business Online. Office 365 ProPlus, and Office 365 Enterprise E3 include the full Skype for Business (Lync) application, which include additional features including advanced telephony support, archiving &amp; compliance features. A Skype for Business Online license must be assigned for each user. For more information on Lync Basic features, see [Skype for Business Online client comparison tables](https://technet.microsoft.com/en-us/library/gg425836%28v=ocs.15%29.aspx). </span></span><br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-6015"><sup>2</sup> Skype 商務 Online 計劃 1 使用者可參與共用工作階段經由依商務 Online 計劃 2 使用者 Skype。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-6015"><sup>2</sup> A Skype for Business Online Plan 1 user may participate in a sharing session if they are invited by a Skype for Business Online Plan 2 user.</span></span> 
<br/> <span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-6016">封存的商務 online Skype 倚賴 Exchange 就地保留功能，不包含在此計劃<sup>3</sup> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-6016"><sup>3</sup> Archiving for Skype for Business Online depends upon the Exchange In-Place Hold feature, which is not included in this plan.</span></span>

## <a name="project-online-features"></a><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-6019">Project Online 功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-6019">Project Online features</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-6021">下表列出可用於由 21Vianet 方案運作之 Office 365 的 Exchange Online 保護 (EOP) Project Online 功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-6021">The following table lists the Project Online features that are available across Office 365 operated by 21Vianet plans.</span></span>
  
> [!NOTE]

## <a name="follow-on-wechat"></a><span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-6566">在 WeChat 上關注我們</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-6566">Follow on WeChat</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-6567"><a name="BM10_ProjectOnline"> </a></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-6567"></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1d8ba-6568">掃描此 QR 碼，在 WeChat 上關注我們的討論區，並取得由 21Vianet 提供的 Office 365 的最新更新。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1d8ba-6568">Scan this QR code to follow discussions on WeChat and get the latest updates for Office 365 operated by 21Vianet.</span></span> 
  
![WeChat 的 QR 碼](../media/8f6064e6-ccf3-4050-97e3-619058b3c806.jpg)
